                        <div data-reactid="332">
                         <li data-reactid="333"><p data-reactid="334">What a great little place! Literally next to Culver Studios (where Gone With the Wind was filmed) and minutes from the Sony lot, the studio's located in a quiet neighborhood with almost no street traffic. Everything inside is brand new. It's a great place to chill after a day packed with business meetings. Corinne will be my first call next time I'm back!</p><span data-reactid="335">Caroline</span><span data-reactid="336">2016-05-21T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="337"><p data-reactid="338">I had the pleasure of staying here for a month on an extended business trip. Corrine's place exceeded all expectations. It's very clean, well-appointed, comfortable. The front yard is fenced off, providing much appreciated privacy. I enjoyed just sitting out on the patio at night with a cup of tea. There is a smart TV in the apartment, so if you have a Netflix, Hulu, HBO Go or Amazon account, you can binge away after a long day. Location is very central. Downtown Culver is just 10 mins walk, and has a Trader Joe's, Arclight Cinema, hair saloon, many restaurants. Another 5 mins walk takes you to the Culver City metro, from which you can head to Santa Monica or go to Downtown LA. Plenty of Uber drivers seem to service this area --- I never had to wait more than 5 mins for a pickup. Corrine and her husband Sean were both great hosts --- very respectful of privacy yet never more than a text message away if I needed any assistance. I will miss this home away from home. </p><span data-reactid="339">Steven</span><span data-reactid="340">2016-10-06T00:00:00Z</span></li>
